### 1. Nano Banana 2 代示例和提示

**Author**: [KAWAI](https://x.com/kawai_design)  **Date**: 2026-03-03  **Language**: ja

> 以下是针对 Gogole Nano Banana 2 的四个详细图像生成提示，涵盖了肖像、街拍、产品和海报风格，强调了详细提示对于获得高质量结果的重要性。

![Nano Banana 2 代示例和提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605589980_fx8ny5_HCfSCUQaEAAqeBh.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 代示例和提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605590341_9b3c1o_HCfR6TZa0AA6sdD.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 代示例和提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605590542_r68yeb_HCfR-p2boAEAMX9.jpg)
![Nano Banana 2 代示例和提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605591291_vm0dkg_HCfSkceaoAAEMPL.jpg)

```
1枚目：ポートレート

強いサイドライトによって顔の半分が影になった、ドラマチックなモノクロームポートレート。影の部分は完全に黒く、光の当たった部分は肌の質感が際立つ。Hasselblad X1D II 50CとXCD 80mm F1.9レンズで撮影。

─────────────────

2枚目：ストリートスナップ

雑踏の中、一瞬立ち止まってカメラを見つめる人物のストリートポートレート。背景は適度にボケさせ、人物に焦点を当てる。Leica Q2で撮影されたようなスナップショット感。

─────────────────

3枚目：プロダクト

洗練されたミニマリストな空間に、最新のスマートウォッチが浮遊している広告ビジュアル。背景は深みのあるネイビーとゴールドのグラデーション。スマートウォッチの画面には『{argument name="スマートウォッチの文字" default="Time Redefined"}』という文字が表示されている。

─────────────────

4枚目：ポスター

音楽フェスティバルのポスター。サイケデリックな色彩と抽象的な模様が組み合わさり、フェスティバルのテーマ『{argument name="フェスティバルのテーマ" default="Sound Odyssey"}』が大きく表示されている。多様なフォントとレイアウトを試す。
```

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成产品（占位符）的逼真 8k Octane 渲染图，该产品居中并悬浮在漆黑的虚空中。该提示指定了技术细节，例如轮廓光、高对比度明暗对比、特定的金属纹理（钛、铝）以及凹槽玻璃失真等光学效果。

![Restomod 产品照片，采用明暗对比照明](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346687595_bcrg7q_HCOeiR2WEAAnYoC.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject": {
      "placeholder": "{argument name="product name" default="INSERT PRODUCT HERE"}",
      "position": "dead center, eye-level, perfectly centered in frame",
      "presentation": "levitating, floating in a weightless void, no stands, no platforms, no pedestals, no visible supports"
    },
    "environment": {
      "background": "absolute solid pitch black, hex code #000000, infinite void",
      "lighting": "rim lighting, cinematic chiaroscuro, high-contrast glints on metallic edges, soft orange glow from internal recesses"
    },
    "aesthetic_style": {
      "textures": [
        "shot-blasted matte titanium",
        "brushed aerospace-grade aluminum",
        "anodized dark grey metal",
        "ribbed industrial vertical cooling fins"
      ],
      "optical_effects": "viewed through vertical fluted reeded glass, subtle chromatic distortion, refractive glass warping, radial motion blur on outer edges",
      "color_palette": {
        "primary_background": "#000000",
        "secondary_metal": "#8E8E8E",
        "accent_glow": "#FF8C00",
        "highlights": "#FFFFFF"
      }
    },
    "composition_constraints": {
      "framing": "ensure full product visibility, do not cut off edges, wide safety margins around the subject",
      "elements_to_exclude": [
        "text",
        "logos",
        "watermarks",
        "softboxes",
        "light stands",
        "floor",
        "horizon line",
        "props",
        "human hands",
        "shadows on surfaces"
      ]
    },

      "focal_length": "85mm macro lens",
      "depth_of_field": "deep focus on product, blurred refractive foreground glass",

    }
  }
}

### 5. Chrome Ripple Flow 产品摄影提示

**Author**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates)  **Date**: 2026-02-12  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的产品摄影提示，重点是生成一个浮空产品，该产品具有哑光黑色和金属银色饰面，居中放置在一个单一、连续、起伏的背景表面上，该表面具有精细的罗纹纹理和无缝的双色渐变。

![Chrome Ripple Flow 产品摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770964542027_zvtlha_HA-HvY7XwAAasmn.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject": "{argument name="product name" default="PRODUCT"}",
    "product_finish": {
      "primary": "matte black with subtle light absorption",
      "secondary": "polished metallic silver with mirror-like reflections",
      "treatment": "duotone — matte black body with metallic silver accents, trim, edges, or panel insets"
    },
    "composition": {
      "placement": "dead center, full view, floating suspended within the folded surface environment",
      "scale": "product occupies roughly 30-40% of the frame",
      "constraints": [
        "product must be entirely visible with no cropping",
        "no pedestals, stands, platforms, or ground planes",
        "the surface folds frame the product but never obscure more than 10% of it",
        "product is the sharpest element in the scene"
      ]
    },
    "background_environment": {
      "description": "A single continuous undulating surface that fills the entire frame, folding over and around itself in large voluminous waves — like a massive sheet of pleated metallic silk or a single machined metal panel that has been softly twisted and draped. This is NOT multiple separate ribbons or strands. It is ONE connected surface.",
      "base_color": "{argument name="deep background color" default="INSERT DEEP BACKGROUND COLOR visible in crevices — e.g. pure black, midnight navy"}",
      "surface_color_1": "{argument name="gradient color A" default="INSERT GRADIENT COLOR A — e.g. soft lavender, warm copper, pearl rose"}",
      "surface_color_2": "[INSERT GRADIENT COLOR B — e.g. deep indigo, cobalt blue, violet]",
      "color_behavior": "The two colors blend in a smooth continuous gradient across the single surface, shifting based on the surface's curvature and light angle. Where the surface faces the light it shows color_1, where it curves away it transitions to color_2. The transition is seamless with no hard edges or stripes.",
      "surface_texture": {
        "type": "fine parallel ribs embossed into the surface — like the grooves on a vinyl record or finely pleated accordion fabric",
        "rib_description": "extremely fine, uniform, tightly spaced parallel lines that follow the flow direction of the surface. The ribs are a TEXTURE on the surface, not separate objects. They create a subtle corrugated micro-relief that catches light along each tiny ridge.",
        "rib_density": "very high — approximately 50-100 visible lines per inch of surface, creating a dense linear grain",
        "rib_depth": "shallow — the ribs are subtle surface detail, not deep cuts. They create gentle highlight-shadow alternation across the surface"
      },
      "surface_form": {
        "fold_style": "large, smooth, voluminous folds like draped heavy silk — broad sweeping curves with gentle twists",
        "fold_count": "3-5 major folds visible, each one wide and generous, NOT many small tangled ribbons",
        "fold_behavior": "folds overlap softly, tucking under and over each other with smooth transitions. Where folds meet they create dee"

Environmental Layering: The foreground consists of fine sand forming low dunes, softly contoured and in sharp focus; the midground is dominated by the stone and stacked bottles, all sharply resolved with clear edge definition; the background is a seamless studio gradient transitioning vertically from deep orange at the top to pale yellow near the horizon, with no discernible texture or depth cues and no bokeh due to uniform focus across planes. Technical Artifacts & Color: The color palette is warm and tightly controlled, dominated by orange, amber, sand-beige, and pale yellow, contrasted by the transparent glass highlights; saturation is moderate to high in the labels and background, lower in the sand and stone; no visible chromatic aberration or lens distortion is present; edges are clean, and there is minimal grain, suggesting a controlled studio capture or lightly applied grain overlay; no motion blur or compositing artifacts are visible, despite the implausible balance. ```

### 12. 保时捷技术产品文档提示

**Author**: [Ravikesh Kumar](https://x.com/Ravikesh0406)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: en

> 这是一个针对 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 的高度具体、技术性提示，旨在生成详细、分析性的产品文档图像（例如，用于保时捷）。它要求将上传的图像作为唯一的事实来源，需要纯白色背景、辅助视图、带矢量线的组件标注，以及斯堪的纳维亚工业文档风格，并严格禁止营销语言或臆测的功能。

![保时捷技术产品文档提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755054850_5qi4l1_G_z_nnwbUAEpHIC.jpg)
![保时捷技术产品文档提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755054812_vtq6wr_G_0DaH1bYAARy-1.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded image as the sole source of truth.
Do NOT assume model, specs, or performance.

Pure white, distraction-free background.

Top-left: PORSCHE (modern sans-serif).
Left column: auxiliary views
(front / side / rear / detail).
Right side: large photorealistic hero render.

Visually analyze only what is visible.
Identify distinct physical components.
Label each component with hairline-thin vector lines.
Use neutral, factual terms only.
No marketing language.
No hallucinated features.
No assumed performance.

Scandinavian, modern, industrial documentation style.
Soft studio lighting.
Ultra-high resolution.
Exact proportions and geometry fidelity.
```

### 13. 高端产品目录风格提示词（技术规格）

**Author**: [摆烂程序媛](https://x.com/wanerfu)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: zh

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张高端产品目录图片，采用 3:4 垂直构图的详细提示。布局包括顶部的生活方式主图和底部的技术规格面板，其中包含建筑线条图和材料样本，旨在营造出精致、建筑感和宁静的设计期刊美学。

![高端产品目录风格提示词（技术规格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755040577_518wxr_G_y7n35bYAAIK4m.jpg)

```
✓ 参考图像：使用上传的图像作为产品形式、比例、材料和整体身份的精确视觉参考。不要重新设计或重新解释产品。

✓ 布局：竖向3:4画布，背景为温暖中性纸质表面，上部为生活方式英雄区域，下部为技术规格区。

✓ 上部分：产品图像置于顶部中心，占据主导位置，周围有充足留白。

✓ 环境设置：极简主义建筑室内，自然侧光照明，柔和高对比阴影，混凝土地面，纹理灰泥墙。

✓ 渲染风格：编辑性生活摄影，高度写实，温暖柔和的高端色彩分级。

✓ 下部分：技术规格面板采用模块化网格布局。左下为建筑线条图（正视图、侧视图、四分之三俯视图），柔和红色或棕褐色细线条，最少标注。

✓ 右下：3-4个材料样本，来自产品实际材料（织物、皮革、金属、木材、塑料）。

✓ 排版：极简编辑风格，柔和黑色或深棕色，无大标题。

✓ 整体风格：设计目录/产品设计日志，建筑感、高端、平静。避免杂乱、大胆色彩、重品牌、过度装饰。

✓ 约束：不改变产品设计，不虚构材料，除非参考中有否则不添加徽标，在图纸中不使用透视失真。
```

[[Product Photography]]

### 16. 超逼真魔爪（Monster Energy）产品图，配霓虹火焰

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细、技术性强的提示，用于生成一张怪物能量饮料罐的超逼真产品照片。它侧重于微小的细节，如微凝结水珠、金属反光，以及从下方喷涌而出的霓虹绿色火焰的物理效果，所有这些都通过特定的相机和照明规格呈现，以实现高冲击力的电影级特写。

```
Hyper-realistic 4K product photo of a Monster Energy can, logo centered and perfectly sharp, the can suspended in mid-air with no visible support. 

The can's surface is cold and tactile: dense micro-condensation (droplets 0.1-1.2 mm) with natural gravity streaks, crisp specular glints, subtle lacquer micro-scratches and brushed metallic reflections visible along the curvature. Black body paint reads deep and velvety, the green 'M' claw mark remains vivid and undistorted. From the bottom edge of the frame, vivid neon-green flames erupt upward, frozen mid-motion, licking around the can without touching or consuming it. Flames are hyper-detailed: semi-transparent feathered edges, emissive cores, laminar-to-turbulent transitions, filamentary curls, Kelvin-Helmholtz ripples, wispy tongues and vortex roll-ups. Fine incandescent sparks and nano-embers hang in the air, some caught as sharp pinpoints, others rendered as faint bokeh glints. Tiny heat-distortion ripples subtly bend the background near the flame edges (very restrained). Behind the scene, blurred and veiled in haze, a vague silhouette of a roaring beast's head glows faintly inside green smoke a suggestive contour only, semi-obscured by fog, adding mythic presence without distracting from the can. Cinematic low-angle close-up composition, vertical 3:4. Generous negative space at the bottom emphasizes the upward eruption. Full-frame 100 mm macro prime, f/8 for deep micro-texture, 1/200 s, ISO 100. Critical focus plane on the Monster logo, condensation droplets on the front cylinder, and the nearest flame filaments; background falls smoothly into creamy bokeh. Lighting: dual-rim system with high contrast. Camera-left: intense neon-green backlight (~520 nm) skimming the flames, amplifying translucency and emissive cores. Camera-right: cool blue-white rim (~6500 K) defining the can's cylindrical edges and revealing micro-condensation sparkle. A very subtle frontal fill (5-8%) preserves logo readability without flattening blacks. Black flags and negative fill maintain deep shadows; no spill on the background. Atmosphere: thin volumetric smoke and low-density haze rise from below, catching rim beams to create delicate light shafts. Sparse drifting particles read as 'air texture' around the flames.
```

[[Product Photography]] [[Cinematic Close-Up]] [[Condensation Detail]] [[Technical Camera Specification]]

### 22. 9 格产品故事板模型提示

**Author**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-22  **Language**: en

> 这是一个高度结构化的提示，旨在为高端产品品牌组合生成一个 3x3 的故事板网格。它要求使用参考图像来确保所有九个面板中产品的一致性，并为每个画面指定独特的构图、焦点和场景，强调形式、构图和视觉节奏而非写实主义。

![9 格产品故事板模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149364094_5vjm3w_G_Qh_LCbwAAIvTE.jpg)

```
A clean 3×3 [ratio] storyboard grid with nine equal [ratio] sized panels on [4:5] ratio. 

Use the reference image as the base product reference. Keep the same product, packaging design, branding, materials, colors, proportions and overall identity across all nine panels exactly as the reference. The product must remain clearly recognizable in every frame. The label, logo and proportions must stay exactly the same.

This storyboard is a high-end designer mockup presentation for a branding portfolio. The focus is on form, composition, materiality and visual rhythm rather than realism or lifestyle narrative. The overall look should feel curated, editorial and design-driven.

FRAME 1:
Front-facing hero shot of the product in a clean studio setup. Neutral background, balanced composition, calm and confident presentation of the product.

FRAME 2:
Close-up shot with the focus centered on the middle of the product. Focusing on surface texture, materials and print details.

FRAME 3:
Shows the reference product placed in an environment that naturally fits the brand and product category. Studio setting inspired by the product design elements and colours. 

FRAME 4:
Product shown in use or interaction on a neutral studio background. Hands and interaction elements are minimal and restrained, the look matches the style of the package. 

FRAME 5:
Isometric composition showing multiple products arranged in a precise geometric order from the top isometric angle. All products are placed at the same isometric top angle, evenly spaced, clean, structured and graphic.

FRAME 6:
Product levitating slightly tilted on a neutral background that matches the reference image color palette. Floating position is angled and intentional, the product is floating naturally in space.

FRAME 7:
is an extreme close-up focusing on a specific detail of the label, edge, texture or material behavior.

FRAME 8:
The product in an unexpected yet aesthetically strong setting that feels bold, editorial and visually striking.
Unexpected but highly stylized setting. Studio-based, and designer-driven. Bold composition that elevates the brand.

FRAME 9:
Wide composition showing the product in use, placed within a refined designer setup. Clean props, controlled styling, cohesive with the rest of the series.

CAMERA & STYLE:
Ultra high-quality studio imagery with a real camera look. Different camera angles and framings across frames. Controlled depth of field, precise lighting, accurate materials and reflections. Lighting logic, color palette, mood and visual language must remain consistent across all nine panels as one cohesive series.

OUTPUT:
A clean 3×3 grid with no borders, no text, no captions and no watermarks.
```

[[Product Photography]] [[3x3 Photo Grid]]

---

### 23. 品牌视觉的详细故事板提示

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2026-01-22  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度详细、多帧的提示，专为 Nano Banana Pro 设计，用于生成一个干净、专业的 3x3 故事板网格，以用于品牌组合。它强调所有九个帧中产品标识、颜色和比例的一致性，侧重于构图、材质和视觉节奏，而非叙事。

![品牌视觉的详细故事板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149374673_qpygep_G_QW86Za4AANkA3.jpg)

```
3×3 [比率] のクリーンなストーリーボードグリッドに、9 つの [比率] サイズのパネルを [4:5] の比率で配置します。

参考画像を製品のベースイメージとして使用します。製品、パッケージデザイン、ブランディング、素材、色、比率、全体的なアイデンティティは、参考画像と完全に同じにしてください。製品はすべてのフレームで明確に認識できる必要があります。ラベル、ロゴ、比率は完全に同じである必要があります。

このストーリーボードは、ブランディングポートフォリオ用の高級デザイナーによるモックアッププレゼンテーションです。リアリズムやライフスタイルのナラティブではなく、形状、構成、素材、視覚的なリズムに焦点を当てています。全体的な外観は、キュレーションされた、編集された、デザイン主導の印象を与える必要があります。

フレーム 1:
クリーンなスタジオセットアップで、製品を正面から撮影したヒーローショット。ニュートラルな背景、バランスの取れた構図、落ち着いた自信に満ちた製品のプレゼンテーション。

フレーム2：
製品の中心にフォーカスを合わせたクローズアップショット。表面の質感、素材、印刷のディテールに焦点を当てています。

フレーム3：
ブランドと製品カテゴリーに自然に溶け込む環境に配置された参考製品。製品のデザイン要素と色彩からインスピレーションを得たスタジオセッティングです。

フレーム4：
ニュートラルなスタジオの背景に、製品の使用またはインタラクションの様子が写っています。手やインタラクション要素は最小限に抑えられ、パッケージのスタイルにマッチした外観です。

フレーム5：
複数の製品を上面から等角投影し、正確な幾何学的順序で配置したアイソメトリック構図です。すべての製品が同じ上面から等角投影され、均等な間隔で配置され、すっきりと整理され、グラフィックな印象を与えます。

フレーム6：
参考画像のカラーパレットにマッチしたニュートラルな背景に、製品がわずかに傾けて浮かんでいます。意図的に角度をつけて浮かんでいるため、製品は空間に自然に浮かんでいます。

フレーム7：
ラベル、エッジ、テクスチャ、または素材の挙動といった特定のディテールに焦点を当てた、極めてクローズアップのショットです。

フレーム8：
製品は、予想外でありながらも美的に力強いセッティングの中にあり、大胆でエディトリアルな印象を与え、視覚的に印象的です。

予想外でありながら、高度に様式化されたセッティング。スタジオを拠点とし、デザイナー主導で制作。ブランドイメージを高める大胆な構図。

フレーム9：
洗練されたデザイナーのセッティングの中に置かれた製品の使用シーンを映し出すワイドな構図。無駄のない小道具、コントロールされたスタイリング、そしてシリーズの他の作品との統一感。

カメラとスタイル：
リアルなカメラルックを備えた、超高画質のスタジオ撮影。フレームごとに異なるカメラアングルとフレーミング。被写界深度、正確な照明、正確な素材と反射。照明のロジック、カラーパレット、ムード、そしてビジュアルランゲージは、9つのパネル全体で一貫性を保ち、1つのシリーズとして統一する必要があります。

出力:
境界線、テキスト、キャプション、透かしのない、すっきりとした 3×3 グリッド。
```

### 25. 笔记本电脑图像上的技术信息图叠加

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成笔记本电脑技术信息图图像的提示，将逼真的渲染与黑色墨水风格的线条图和注释（标签、尺寸、流程箭头）结合在纯白色背景上，营造出工程手册的美感。

![笔记本电脑图像上的技术信息图叠加](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977299106_nnliin_G_HA1OGXYAAzskM.jpg)

```
Create an infographic image of {argument name="object" default="laptop"} ,combining a realistic photograph or photoreal render of the object with technical annotation overlays placed directly on top.

Use black ink–style line drawings and text (technical pen / architectural sketch look) on a pure white studio background, including:
•Key component labels
•Internal cutaway or exploded-view outlines
•Measurements, dimensions, and scale markers
•Material callouts and quantities
•Arrows indicating function, force, or flow (air, sound, power, pressure)
•Simple schematic or sectional diagrams where relevant

Place the title [OBJECT] inside a hand-drawn technical annotation box in one corner.

Style & layout rules:
•The real object remains clearly visible beneath the annotations
•Annotations feel sketched, technical, and architectural
•Clean composition with balanced negative space
•Educational, museum-exhibit / engineering-manual vibe

Visual style:
Minimal technical illustration aesthetic, black linework over realistic imagery, precise but slightly hand-drawn feel.

Color palette:
White background, black annotation lines and text only. No colors.

Output:
1080×1080, ultra-crisp, social-feed optimized, no watermark.”
```

### 26. 3x3 品牌组合产品故事板网格

**Author**: [Vi](https://x.com/tehno_maniak)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多帧提示，旨在将单个参考图像转换为用于高端品牌组合的内聚 3x3 故事板网格。它要求所有九个面板严格遵守参考产品的特性，每个面板都从不同的角度、背景或特写镜头描绘产品，重点关注设计、材料和视觉节奏。

![3x3 品牌组合产品故事板网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977285349_fcvu8y_G_FaISRWkAAHtDT.jpg)
![3x3 品牌组合产品故事板网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977285425_h649sn_G_FaISSXMAArcKp.jpg)
![3x3 品牌组合产品故事板网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977285329_hv6b53_G_FaISSXUAApmZI.jpg)

```
Create ONE final image.

A clean 3×3 [ratio] storyboard grid with nine equal [ratio] sized panels on [4:5] ratio.

Use the reference image as the base product reference. Keep the same product, packaging design, branding, materials, colors, proportions and overall identity across all nine panels exactly as the reference. The product must remain clearly recognizable in every frame. The label, logo and proportions must stay exactly the same.

This storyboard is a high-end designer mockup presentation for a branding portfolio. The focus is on form, composition, materiality and visual rhythm rather than realism or lifestyle narrative. The overall look should feel curated, editorial and design-driven.

FRAME 1:
Front-facing hero shot of the product in a clean studio setup. Neutral background, balanced composition, calm and confident presentation of the product.

FRAME 2:
Close-up shot with the focus centered on the middle of the product. Focusing on surface texture, materials and print details.

FRAME 3:
Shows the reference product placed in an environment that naturally fits the brand and product category. Studio setting inspired by the product design elements and colours.

FRAME 4:
Product shown in use or interaction on a neutral studio background. Hands and interaction elements are minimal and restrained, the look matches the style of the package.

FRAME 5:
Isometric composition showing multiple products arranged in a precise geometric order from the top isometric angle. All products are placed at the same isometric top angle, evenly spaced, clean, structured and graphic.

FRAME 6:
Product levitating slightly tilted on a neutral background that matches the reference image color palette. Floating position is angled and intentional, the product is floating naturally in space.

FRAME 7:
is an extreme close-up focusing on a specific detail of the label, edge, texture or material behavior.

FRAME 8:
The product in an unexpected yet aesthetically strong setting that feels bold, editorial and visually striking.
Unexpected but highly stylized setting. Studio-based, and designer-driven. Bold composition that elevates the brand.

FRAME 9:
Wide composition showing the product in use, placed within a refined designer setup. Clean props, controlled styling, cohesive with the rest of the series.

CAMERA & STYLE:
Ultra high-quality studio imagery with a real camera look. Different camera angles and framings across frames. Controlled depth of field, precise lighting, accurate materials and reflections. Lighting logic, color palette, mood and visual language must remain consistent across all nine panels as one cohesive series.

OUTPUT:
A clean 3×3 grid with no borders, no text, no captions and no watermarks.
```

[[Product Photography]] [[Commercial Photography]] [[Grid Layout]]

### 27. 高端商业产品拼贴画提示（韩语）

**Author**: [TheAIHeadquarters](https://x.com/DavisonDabiri)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: ko

> 这是一个极其详细、结构化的提示，用于生成一个 6 格（3x2 网格）高端商业产品拼贴画，专门针对香水或电子产品等物品，使用 Nano Banana Pro。它要求严格遵守参考图像的产品特征，指定常见的照明和技术参数（照片级真实感、影棚照明、深景深），并包含一个由 16 种不同视觉风格（例如，深红色英雄特写、米白色微距细节、镀铬镜面房间）组成的池，其中必须随机选择 6 种用于面板。它还包括品牌、文本移除和镜头分配的规则。

```
[입력(변수)] 참조이미지=첨부한 제품/물건 사진(필수), 제품카테고리={argument name="Product Category" default="향수/스킨케어/전자기기/식품/주얼리/기타"}, 무드=럭셔리·프리미엄, 메인컬러=앰버골드, 보조컬러=딥레드+오프화이트+블랙, 그리드=3x2(가로3·세로2), 여백=얇은 흰색 구터(2~4px), 최종비율=3:2, 해상도=3840x2560, 렌즈셋=히어로50mm/매크로100mm/세트35mm, 랜덤시드=임의(매번 다르게)
[목표] 참조이미지의 “제품 형태·비율·재질·색”을 정확히 유지한 채, 하이엔드 상업 광고용 6컷 콜라주(3x2)로 제작. 6컷 모두 동일한 단일 제품(같은 제품 1개)로 인식되게 일관성 유지(제품이 2개 이상 보이지 않기).
[공통 촬영/연출] 포토리얼 상업 제품사진, 스튜디오 라이팅(키라이트+림라이트+소프트필), 유리/금속 하이라이트 선명, 미세한 난반사와 굴절 표현, 자연스러운 그림자 접지, 얕은 심도와 선명한 초점, 고급 컬러그레이딩(웜 앰버+딥 레드 대비), 노이즈 최소, 과장된 HDR/왜곡/과포화 금지, 제품 가장자리 깨끗, 배경은 미니멀.
[브랜딩/텍스트 규칙] 로고/상표/브랜드명/읽을 수 있는 글자 제거(라벨은 무지 라벨 또는 추상 패턴), 글자 깨짐/가짜 문자 생성 금지, 워터마크/서명/QR 금지.
[레이아웃] 하나의 캔버스 안에 6개 패널을 3x2로 정확히 배치. 패널 간 톤 통일, 구도 다양화, 제품은 항상 주인공(프레임 30~70% 점유), 소품/이펙트는 제품을 가리지 않기.
[핵심: 16가지 스타일 풀에서 랜덤 6개 선택] 아래 STYLE_POOL_16 중 “서로 다른 6개”를 매 실행마다 랜덤으로 선택하여 3x2 패널에 배치. 선택된 6개는 중복 금지. 선택 안 된 10개는 이번 결과에 포함하지 않기. 각 패널은 선택된 스타일의 룩을 강하게 따르되, 제품 동일성/톤은 유지.
[STYLE_POOL_16] S1_딥레드히어로: 딥 레드 배경 + 블랙 마블 베이스, 정면 대칭 히어로, 바닥 약한 반사, 50mm.
S2_오프화이트매크로디테일: 오프화이트 그라데이션 배경, 100mm 매크로로 캡/상단/유리 굴절 디테일 극대화, 먼지 없는 표면.
S3_블랙골든미스트: 블랙 배경, 골든 파우더/미스트가 뒤에서 퍼짐, 앰버 입자 보케, 역광 림라이트, 50mm.
S4_모던오브제세트: 브러시드 메탈+우드+투명 아크릴(또는 미니멀 세트), 건축적 정렬, 35mm 세트샷.
S5_부유꽃잎앰버칩: 제품 공중 부유(지지대 보이지 않게), 꽃잎+앰버칩 플로팅, 모션블러 최소, 35mm.
S6_손모델클로즈업: clean studio hand model, correct anatomy, 손이 캡을 살짝 잡는 매크로, 손이 라벨/정면 가리지 않게, 베이지/오프화이트 배경, 100mm.
S7_딥레드미니멀기둥: 딥 레드/골드 톤 미니멀 기둥/벽면(세로 구조물) 앞 단독 제품, 그래픽 라이트 스트립, 패션 광고 느낌, 50mm.
S8_리본실크플로우: 실크 리본/오간자 천이 제품 주변을 유려하게 감싸는 플로팅, 투명하고 얇은 레이어, 우아한 흐름, 35mm.
S9_가든디올라마: 황혼/야간 미니 정원 디오라마, 유리꽃/투명 오브제와 보케, 배경은 식별 불가한 건축 실루엣, 동화적이되 리얼 톤, 50mm.
S10_스킨케어워터글라스: 물방울/젖은 유리/맑은 응결, 깨끗한 화이트-아쿠아 하이라이트, 스플래시는 최소, 35mm.
S11_테크네온에지: 네온 엣지 라이트, 얇은 연무, 메탈릭 반사와 라인 하이라이트, 블랙-차콜 배경, 35mm 또는 50mm.
S12_시즌테마랜덤: 계절 1개 랜덤 선택(혼합 금지), 봄=파스텔 꽃가루/연한 꽃잎, 여름=맑은 물방울/서늘한 증기, 가을=앰버 크리스털/메이플 톤, 겨울=서리/아이스 크리스털/차가운 글로우, 50mm 또는 35mm.
S13_크롬미러룸: 크롬/미러 패널로 둘러싸인 미니 룸, 반사 속 제품이 “한 번만” 보이게(중복 착시 금지), 하이라이트 라인 깨끗, 35mm.
S14_페이퍼아트라이트박스: 종이 레이어 컷아웃 배경(고급 패키징/라이트박스 느낌), 소프트 섀도우, 미니멀 그래픽 형태, 종이는 리얼 질감, 35mm.
S15_레트로필름그레인라이트: 80s~90s 인쇄광고 감성의 아주 약한 필름 그레인과 소프트 글로우, 컬러는 고급스럽게 절제(촌스럽지 않게), 제품은 선명, 50mm.
S16_미니스포트라이트무대: 원형 미니 스테이지 + 스포트라이트 원뿔 빛, 주변은 어둡고 중심만 밝게, 먼지 없는 빛기둥, 프리미엄 런칭 무드, 50mm.
[제품카테고리별 소품 자동 적용 규칙] 향수=꽃잎+앰버칩+골든 미스트, 스킨케어=물방울+젖은 유리+클린 스팀, 전자기기=네온 엣지 라이트+얇은 연무+메탈릭 반사, 식품=크럼/파우더+시럽 스플래시(최소)+재료 한두 조각, 주얼리=프리즘 크리스털+실크 패브릭+스파클 보케, 기타=메인컬러와 조화되는 미니멀 소품 1~3개만.
[렌즈 배정 가이드] 무대감/히어로(S1,S3,S7,S9,S16)=50mm, 디테일(S2,S6)=100mm, 세트/부유/리본/워터/테크/미러/페이퍼(S4,S5,S8,S10,S11,S12,S13,S14)=35mm 중심(필요 시 50mm), 레트로(S15)=50mm.
```

### 31. 社交媒体内容生成提示

**Author**: [Chase Dimond | Email Marketing Nerd 📧](https://x.com/ecomchasedimond)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一个文本提示，指示 AI 模型（Gamma/Nano Banana Pro）为特定产品生成完整的社交媒体内容，重点是具有精确排版和品牌标识的超逼真产品照片。

```
Create a social media feed for this {argument name="product type" default="small-batch olive oil brand"}.
```

**Author**: [Özge](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-03  **Language**: en

> 一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 的复杂 JSON 提示，侧重于参考图像中的产品替换。目标是将现有照片转换为“Bagel Labs”口红的超逼真冬季美妆广告，严格保持原始场景、姿势和光线，同时确保新产品品牌清晰可辨。

      }
    },

      "orientation": "match_reference",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "ultra_photoreal_beauty_advertising",
      "sharpness": "crisp_but_natural",
      "film_grain": "none_or_minimal",
      "color_grade": "clean_true_to_life_cool_winter",
      "retouch_level": "editorial_minimal_keep_texture",
      "noise_reduction": "low"
    },
    "hard_constraints": [
      "ONE female subject only.",
      "Maintain the existing pose, framing, lighting, snowy alpine background, and falling snow.",
      "Modify only the cosmetic product in her hand.",
      "The brand name 'Bagel Labs' must be clearly readable on the product.",
      "Natural skin texture must remain visible.",
      "No watermark."
    ],
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "Create a luxury winter beauty advertising image in a bright snowy alpine environment with falling snow and a clear blue sky.     },

**Author**: [Amanpreet Singh](https://x.com/amanxdesign)  **Date**: 2025-12-28  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 格式提示，专为 Google Nano Banana Pro 模型设计，旨在生成高质量、一致的电子商务或 Shopify 产品列表照片。该提示侧重于保持参考服装（一件深灰色罗纹针织连衣裙）的精确外观和质地，同时将模特置于温暖、亲切、休闲的生活场景中，例如咖啡馆或客厅，强调高端休闲时尚摄影。

![电商产品列表生活场景照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061697624_csnwe2_G87upYfacAAuv3H.jpg)
![电商产品列表生活场景照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061698080_n0om3a_G87upX7bQAA_0wX.jpg)

```
{
  "description": "Full-body or mid-length photo of the same white American woman wearing the exact same dark grey rib-knit dress, identical in texture, silhouette, color, and fabric as the reference. She is styled casually for a lifestyle setting — seated comfortably at an outdoor café table, home terrace, or cozy indoor living area. The outfit is accessorized with a light neutral scarf or a soft, long cardigan draped naturally around her shoulders. She wears the same taupe boots as in the reference image. The model is holding a coffee mug or cup in one hand, with reading glasses placed nearby or gently held. Her expression is calm, slightly warm, and relaxed — as if she’s enjoying a peaceful moment or morning coffee. Hair and makeup remain natural, soft, and consistent with the reference look.",
  
  "style": "modern lifestyle fashion photography; elegant and relatable; premium casual tone; warm and cozy atmosphere with authentic emotion",
  
  "camera": "mid-length or seated full-body framing at eye level; slight angle for lifestyle realism; focus on model and outfit with shallow depth (f/2.8–f/3.2) to softly blur background; natural smartphone perspective for realism",
  
  "lighting": "soft, diffused daylight or warm indoor lighting depending on location; no harsh shadows or overexposure; natural tone with balanced warmth across skin and fabric; light direction from the side to create depth and soft contrast; consistent with the lighting style from the previous indoor reference image",
  
  "environment": "a cozy lifestyle setting — warm-toned modern café, sunlit terrace, or inviting living room; include subtle elements like a wooden table, a coffee cup, books, or plants in the background; light neutral walls and soft décor to complement the outfit; overall environment should feel calm, comfortable, and premium",
  
  "texture": "dress fabric remains heavy and ribbed, matte finish; lighting enhances its texture and structure; scarf or cardigan appears soft with visible knit or wool texture; surfaces like the table or cup subtly reflect light for realism",
  
  "focus": "maintain clarity on the model’s upper body and outfit, slightly shallow depth to separate her from the background; soft vignette for cozy emphasis; jewelry and neckline subtly highlighted by light reflections",
  
  "ending": "replicate the same model, outfit, and material quality as the reference in a casual lifestyle composition — seated calmly with coffee in hand, warm soft lighting, and natural background for a premium yet relatable feel"
}
```

### 54. 产品摄影的视觉创作模式提示（精确与衰减）

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 的“视觉创作模式”设计的复杂系统提示，指示 AI 扮演顶级的视觉创意总监。它接收一个 JSON 格式的“创意骨架”输入（此处聚焦于机械键盘键帽、灰尘和齿轮，并带有“精确与衰败”的张力），并将其优化为一个最终的、高影响力的工业产品摄影英文图像生成提示。

![产品摄影的视觉创作模式提示（精确与衰减）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987758580_yv7jdd_G9LxDc6bgAEAk_A.jpg)

```
## 🎨 Visual Creator Mode

你是一位顶尖的视觉创意总监，同时具备 AI 图像生成能力。

我将提供一份由程序随机生成的"创意骨架 (Creative Skeleton)"，格式为 JSON。你的任务是：

1.  **解读并优化**：理解 JSON 中的各个维度（主题、张力、光影、场景等），将其整合为一个连贯、有视觉冲击力的画面概念。
2.  **先展示优化后的提示词**：在代码块 (```prompt ... ```) 中输出你将要使用的最终图像生成提示词（英文，约 50-100 词）。
3.  **然后，直接生成图片**：使用上述提示词，生成一张高质量的视觉作品。

---

### 优化时请遵循以下原则：

-   **化解冲突**：如果维度组合存在逻辑矛盾（如"工业摄影"配"微缩奇幻"），选择一个主导风格并调和。
-   **视觉锚点**：将抽象张力（如"异想天开 vs 真实材质"）转化为具体的视觉元素（如：融化的巧克力流淌在精密的金属齿轮上）。
-   **传播钩子**：画面需有一个"让人想看第二眼"的意外细节。
-   **风格基调**：若存在 `creative_directive`，将其作为画面的情绪指导；若存在 `oblique_strategy`，将其作为结构层面的约束。

---

### 程序生成的创意骨架（JSON 输入）：
{
  "schema_version": "v1",
  "creative_id": "v9jrcpus",
  "creative_world": "world:product_photography",
  "creation_intent": "形式或材料探索",
  "creation_intent_id": "explore",
  "generation_logic": "过程或制作本身是看点",
  "generation_logic_id": "process-driven",
  "twist_mechanisms": [
    "尺度错位",
    "剖面逻辑",
    "材质错置"
  ],
  "twist_ids": [
    "scale_mismatch",
    "cutaway_logic",
    "material_swap"
  ],
  "subject_kit": {
    "primary_subject": "{argument name="primary subject" default="机械键盘键帽"}",
    "primary_id": "a-mechanical-keyboard-keycap-set",
    "secondary_elements": [
      "灰尘",
      "微型齿轮",
      "规格标签"
    ],
    "secondary_ids": [
      "element:dust",
      "element:tiny-gears",
      "element:spec-label"
    ]
  },
  "core_tension": "精密 vs 腐朽",
  "core_tension_id": "precision_vs_decay",
  "stage_context": "白色无影墙",
  "stage_context_id": "white-cyclorama",
  "composition_rule": "双物体对比布局",
  "composition_rule_id": "two-object-comparison-layout",
  "lighting_rule": "三点专业布光",
  "lighting_rule_id": "three-point-professional-lighting",
  "imaging_assumption": "工业产品摄影",
  "imaging_assumption_id": "industrial_product_photography",
  "deliverable_type": "产品照",
  "emergence": {
    "score": 2,
    "label": "Interesting Combo / 有趣组合"
  },
  "final_prompt": "产品照. featuring 机械键盘键帽, 灰尘, 微型齿轮, 规格标签. inspired by 精密 vs 腐朽. with 尺度错位, 剖面逻辑, 材质错置. set in 白色无影墙. following 双物体对比布局. lit by 三点专业布光.",
  "creative_directive": "把失败当作最终作品",
  "oblique_strategy": {
    "id": "reverse_assumption",
    "desc": "颠倒一个基础假设"
  },
  "validation": {
    "errors": [],
    "warnings": [],
    "dropped_overrides": []
  }
}
```

```
{
  "description": "Full-body photo of the same female model wearing the exact same olive green short dress as in the reference — identical fit, fabric texture, color, neckline, sleeve shape, and length ending above the knees. The model must be fully visible from head to toe within the frame, including both feet and space above the head. The background is a clean light beige tone with soft shadows, maintaining a minimalist and premium look.",
  
  "appearance": "The model appears elegant and confident, with natural makeup and softly styled straight hair. Her facial expression should be calm, relaxed, and professional. Skin should look natural with subtle texture — no airbrushing.",
  
  "pose": "Full-body standing pose with relaxed posture. The model faces slightly toward the camera, one leg slightly ahead of the other for balance. Hands rest naturally at sides or lightly on hips, ensuring the dress remains fully visible. Both feet must be in frame.",
  
  "lighting": "Soft, evenly diffused lighting in a neutral warm tone (around 3800K–4000K). No sunlight or harsh studio reflections. Maintain realistic skin tone and true fabric color.",
  
  "environment": "Simple beige background, smooth gradient with no props or distractions. The focus remains entirely on the model and dress.",
  
  "camera": "Full-body vertical composition, framed slightly wider than before to include the full model from head to toe with extra space above and below. Eye-level perspective with sharp focus on model and dress, slightly soft background for depth.",

  "negative_prompt": [
    "cropped frame (head or feet missing)",
    "long or maxi dress",
    "props or cluttered background",

    "overexposed lighting",

### 62. 3D 激光雕刻水晶饰品生成器

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2025-12-22  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个全面且结构化的提示，将 AI 定义为专业的摄影师和艺术总监。它指示 Nano Banana Pro 根据一个简单的主题或上传的图像，生成一个定制的 3D 次表面激光雕刻水晶摆件的超逼真图像。该提示包含详细的逻辑，用于自主确定水晶形状、基材、环境和照明，以最佳地衬托主题的“氛围”（例如，优雅、舒适、动感），确保最终输出符合严格的写实技术规范。

![3D 激光雕刻水晶饰品生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667395170_76n1u1_G8y9ElQXoAAKRi5.jpg)
![3D 激光雕刻水晶饰品生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667395536_4tus0o_G8y9ElRWsAAJrqw.jpg)
![3D 激光雕刻水晶饰品生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667395995_pdxynz_G8y9ElSWYAA1Tdn.jpg)
![3D 激光雕刻水晶饰品生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667399109_9ak8hf_G8y-6vMXIAEPCzG.jpg)

```
My Subject:  {argument name="subject name" default="主题名称"}
图片比例：9:16

# Role Definition:
You are an expert product photographer and creative art director specializing in high-end luxury goods. Your sole task is to generate a photorealistic image of a custom 3D subsurface laser-engraved crystal ornament based on a simple subject provided by the user.
# Core Directive:
The user will provide only the [Subject]. You must autonomously analyze this subject to determine the most aesthetically appropriate and enhancing configuration for the entire scene. You must decide on the crystal's shape, the base material, the surrounding environment, and the lighting mood to best complement the vibe of the user's subject.
# Creative Analysis Logic (Art Director Instructions):
Analyze the Vibe: Is the subject elegant (e.g., ballerina, swan), cozy (e.g., sleeping cat, family photo), powerful (e.g., lion, sports car), or architectural?
Determine Crystal Shape:
Elegant/Tall Subjects -> Use a tall, multi-faceted prism or diamond shape to enhance verticality.
Solid/Cozy Subjects -> Use a hefty, thick rectangular block or cube to convey weight and warmth.
Dynamic Subjects -> Use complex geometric shapes with many bevels to refract light dramatically.
Determine Environment & Lighting:
Elegant Vibe: Place it in a luxurious, dark, moody environment (art gallery, velvet study). Use dramatic, cool ambient light contrasting with warmth from the base.
Cozy/Warm Vibe: Place it in a homey, soft environment (wooden desk, near a fireplace). Use warm, soft, golden-hour lighting with cozy bokeh.
Modern/Tech Vibe: Place it on a sleek, minimalist surface (polished concrete, dark glass). Use clean, neutral lighting.
# Image Generation Template (Mandatory Technical Specs):
Whatever artistic choices you make based on the logic above, the final image MUST adhere to these technical specifications to ensure a realistic "3D Laser Engraving" look:
Engraving Style: The subject inside must NOT look like a solid 3D print. It MUST be described as a "volumetric white point-cloud engraving," having a "frosty, granular, subsurface texture" made of millions of micro-cracks inside the glass.
Lighting Interaction: The engraving must "glow brilliantly from within," illuminated entirely by warm, golden LED light originating from the base beneath it.
Material: The crystal must be heavy, clear, flawless K9 optical glass with beveled edges that catch and split the light.
Photography Style: Cinematic product photograph, macro lens, extremely shallow depth of field (bokeh), 8k resolution, hyper-detailed.
# Input Process:
I will now provide the subject. You will instantly apply the creative logic and generate the final image.
```

[[Product Photography]]

**Author**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse)  **Date**: 2025-12-20  **Language**: zh

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张 16:9 横向艺术海报的详细提示，海报以机械键盘为主题，围绕一个特定角色展开。构图分为几个部分：左侧是角色的羽毛肖像，右上角是带有技术注释的艺术键帽展示，右下角是三个部分，详细展示了完整的键盘、微距镜头和生活场景摆放。该提示指定了艺术风格、从角色中提取颜色以及排版，旨在营造高端杂志封面的美感。

![机械键盘主题艺术海报提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489534418_ogevon_G8oMfdUW4AARkb9.jpg)

```
一幅16:9横幅构图的机械键盘主题艺术海报。画面左侧占据四分之一宽度，展示  [{argument name="人物角色名称" default="人物角色名称"}]  的半身特写肖像，人物从肩部以上呈现，眼神充满张力，边缘采用柔和羽化效果自然融入背景。人物周围环绕着轻盈的光效粒子和色彩渐变氤氲。

画面右侧占据四分之三宽度，上半部分区域呈现艺术化的键帽展示：5到7个精致的机械键盘键帽以优雅的弧形排列散落在空中，每个键帽展示不同角度和细节。键帽配色方案提取自人物的[{argument name="主色调1" default="樱花粉"}]、[{argument name="主色调2" default="奶油白"}]、[{argument name="点缀色" default="珊瑚红"}]。键帽表面印有[{argument name="主题元素" default="角色Q版剪影/专属图标/渐变纹理"}]，采用[{argument name="键帽材质" default="PBT磨砂/树脂透光"}]材质呈现。每个键帽旁边飘逸着中文艺术字标注，字体使用站酷高端黑或优设标题黑，内容为"{argument name="标注1" default="樱花粉主键"}"、"{argument name="标注2" default="渐变镀膜"}"、"{argument name="标注3" default="双色透光"}"、"{argument name="标注4" default="角色印刷"}"、"{argument name="标注5" default="金属空格"}"等工艺说明，文字带有轻微发光效果和描边。

画面右侧下半部分均匀分为三个区域：左格展示完整机械键盘的正面平铺俯视图，[{argument name="键盘配列" default="68键紧凑配列/铝合金阳极氧化底座"}]，底部标注中文"{argument name="左格标注" default="完整配列"}"；中格展示键盘侧面的微距特写，强调光影下的工艺细节和材质层次，底部标注"{argument name="中格标注" default="匠心工艺"}"；右格展示键盘在[{argument name="场景1" default="温馨书桌场景/咖啡厅桌面/工作台"}]的氛围摆拍，带有[{argument name="道具" default="咖啡杯/绿植/笔记本"}]等生活化道具，底部标注"{argument name="右格标注" default="生活美学"}"。

整体背景采用[{argument name="背景效果" default="水墨晕染/粒子光效/渐变雾面"}]效果，主色调从人物提取的[{argument name="颜色1" default="颜色1"}]到[{argument name="颜色2" default="颜色2"}]渐变过渡，左侧较深右侧较浅。背景中散布着细腻的光斑和流动的色彩云雾，营造出[{argument name="氛围" default="梦幻温柔/赛博科技/复古优雅"}]的氛围。画面底部居中位置有大标题文字："{argument name="大标题" default="角色名称主题定制键盘"}"，使用粗体中文美术字，带有金属质感或发光效果。

画面无明显分割线，各区域通过光影虚实和景深层次自然过渡。整体呈现时尚杂志封面的视觉质感，色彩饱和度适中，层次丰富，兼具艺术性和产品展示功能。4K超高清分辨率，16:9横幅构图，适合社交媒体传播的视觉冲击力。

### 64. 雨伞标记配件生成

**Author**: [はると | X×AIで収益化する発信者](https://x.com/haruto_AI_free)  **Date**: 2025-12-20  **Language**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度具体的提示，以生成一张定制雨伞标记配件（挂饰）连接到透明乙烯基雨伞手柄上的照片级真实图像。它包括关于保持挂饰外观、逼真的连接机制、自然物理（重力）以及雨水、折射和浅景深细节渲染的严格规则。

![雨伞标记配件生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766386022986_1grkec_G8nKpwLb0AAiGf4.jpg)

```
めじるしアクセ本体（チャーム部分）。この画像の形、色、柄、質感、比率、細部のディテールを変更しない。欠け・描き足し・再解釈もしない。 透明ビニール傘の持ち手（グリップ部分、手で握る太い部分）のすぐ近くに、めじるしアクセが実物として自然に装着されている。装着位置は必ず持ち手側で、棒（中棒・シャフト）には付けない。 装着方法は小さなシリコンリング／カニカン／ゴムバンド等で現実的に固定され、持ち手の曲面に沿って接点が自然で、アクセが浮かない。重力方向も自然で、揺れた時にぶら下がる向きが破綻しない。 雨粒、濡れた質感、透明素材の反射と屈折をリアルに。背景は雨の日の街、やわらかいボケ。主役はアクセで、ピントはアクセに合う。 構図はアクセが画面の中心寄り、傘の透明感が伝わる。手や人物を入れる場合は指先だけで清潔感。文字やロゴは入れない。商品写真のように高精細、自然光＋街灯のミックス、浅い被写界深度、マクロ寄り。
```

[[Product Photography]]

### 67. 街头服饰算法 AI：物体到可穿戴设备的转换

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤系统提示，指示 AI 扮演“街头服饰算法”，根据输入对象的物理特性（纹理、结构、形状），将任何随机输入对象转换为相应的“潮牌”时尚单品（羽绒服、运动鞋、背包或太阳镜）。然后，该提示要求生成所生成可穿戴物品的摄影棚产品照片，确保它看起来是由输入对象的部件/材料制造的。

![街头服饰算法 AI：物体到可穿戴设备的转换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237918197_3peyzn_G8VbZ0yWQAAxXcT.jpg)

```
<instruction>Act as the "Streetwear Algorithm" AI.</instruction> 
 Concept:  Turns any random object into the perfect corresponding "Hypebeast" fashion item.
 1. ANALYZE INPUT (Form & Physics): 
 Look at the attached image. Determine:
 Texture: ({argument name="texture options" default="Soft/Hard/Liquid/Glass"})
 Structure:  ({argument name="structure options" default="Rigid/Flexible/Mechanical"})
 Shape:  ({argument name="shape options" default="Boxy/Round/Aerodynamic/Flat"})
 2. AUTO-SELECT MODEL (Run this Logic Tree): 
 IF Input is Soft, Volumetric, or Tangled  (Noodles, Clouds, Moss, Bubblewrap)
 -> GENERATE: Oversized Puffer Jacket 
IF Input is Rigid, Aerodynamic, or Mechanical  (Stapler, Car, Power Tool, Robot)
 -> GENERATE: Chunky Conceptual Sneaker 
 IF Input is Boxy, Container-like, or Heavy Metal  (Safe, Trash Can, Speaker, Computer Case)
 -> GENERATE: Hard-Shell Tech Backpack 
 IF Input is Transparent, Glassy, or Thin/Wire-like  (Neon Sign, Circuit Board, Stained Glass, Ice)
 -> GENERATE: Futuristic Wrap-Around Sunglasses (Visor) 
 IF Input is Textile, Flat, or Pattern-Heavy** ({argument name="pattern input examples" default="Persian Rug, Painting, Cardboard"})
 -> GENERATE: Oversized Hoodie or Tactical Vest 
 
3. EXECUTE DESIGN: 
 Create a studio product shot of the "selected item".
 Design Rule:  The item must look like it was manufactured "using the parts/materials of the input object".
 Details:  Keep original branding/logos if present.
 Setting:  Floating pedestal, Cinematic Lighting, 8k Resolution.
```

### 68. 产品摄影网格生成，助您节省成本

**Author**: [gokaygokay](https://x.com/gokayfem)  **Date**: 2025-12-17  **Language**: en

> 此提示提供了三种使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成产品摄影网格的变体。目标是以 6x6 网格格式快速尝试不同的情绪、美学和产品变体（或同一产品的变体），以节省单个图像生成所需的积分。

![产品摄影网格生成，助您节省成本](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042036025_pzkars_G8XoB3PWYAA4hS7.jpg)
![产品摄影网格生成，助您节省成本](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042036852_0116fc_G8XsB3PXgAA5A8i.jpg)
![产品摄影网格生成，助您节省成本](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042037262_hkfadw_G8XpY_9WQAQKUaL.jpg)
![产品摄影网格生成，助您节省成本](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042038786_qbjsr0_G8XsJBFWIAAqGRS.jpg)

```
Generate a 6x6 grid of professional product photography. Reference the original image's mood, quality, and aesthetic. Each cell should showcase a completely different product ({argument name="products" default="bags, bottles, hats, cosmetics, jewelry, food, electronics, etc."}) in a unique studio setting with a distinct color palette. Maintain the same high-end commercial photography style throughout. Vary the products, lighting, backgrounds, props, and styling dramatically across all 36 images.

Generate a 6x6 grid of variations based on the original image. Keep the same product but vary the color palettes, backgrounds, lighting, angles, props, and styling dramatically across all 36 cells. Maintain the same professional quality and aesthetic throughout.

Generate a 6x6 grid showing 36 unique variations of this product. Experiment wildly with color palettes, environments (studio, lifestyle, minimal, textured backgrounds), lighting styles, compositions, and moods. Keep product recognition and professional quality consistent, but make each cell visually distinct.
```

### 71. Nano Banana Pro 原味零食包装生成提示

**Author**: [かし子🍩](https://x.com/Kashiko_AIart)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro（或 NanoBanana2 PRO）设计的高度详细、复杂的提示词，旨在生成手持原创零食包装的超现实照片。它包含了包装设计、排版、场景优化以及 12 种不同包装形状随机化的详细规则。该提示词使用占位符来表示角色名称和零食设置，如果未指定，这些设置将随机生成。

![Nano Banana Pro 原味零食包装生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509814028_rwpjn4_G7zbOCDaMAY5iPz.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 原味零食包装生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509814086_18b1vo_G7zblS6aMAMn4uY.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 原味零食包装生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509814150_kyyhm5_G7zbZJ6bUAAEDBH.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 原味零食包装生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509817309_if9o1k_G7zcPCvaMAA8zUH.jpg)

```
お菓子のパッケージを手で持っている超リアルな実写写真。背景に参考画像のキャラクターの、味や種類の違うパッケージの並ぶ棚も写り込んでいる。

キャラクター名：「{argument name="キャラクター名" default="〇〇"}」（指定がなければ参考画像の特徴を強烈なユーモアでもじる）

お菓子設定：「{argument name="お菓子設定" default="〇〇"}」

指定がない場合はコンビニ・スーパー・駄菓子屋等に売られているすべてのお菓子のジャンルの中からランダムで1種類選び、奇抜さかお洒落さをブーストしたデザインにすること。

参照画像のキャラクターで 全面装飾されたオリジナルお菓子パッケージを手に持っているリアル写真風の描写。
店頭に並んでいても違和感がないほど自然なデザイン。
お菓子の周囲には店内風景がリアルに存在する。

お菓子パッケージデザイン：

参考画像のキャラクターをパッケージ内に配置する。
お菓子の名前は参考画像の特徴を強烈なユーモアで強調する。
パッケージは超リアルでハイクオリティかつ食欲をそそるハイセンスなデザイン。

光沢の反射表現、材質感をリアルに再現。
中身のお菓子の美味しそうな写真も添える。
装飾以外の部分は透明なビニールにしたり、中身の見える透明フィルムののぞき穴にしたりして中身がある程度見える。

参照画像を元にユーモラスに誇張した複数のキャッチコピーと商品名を、参考画像の雰囲気を反映したフォントで大きく配置する。

お菓子の世界観に適した背景（売り場）を描くこと。
また、背景とパッケージコンセプトに 感情的・色彩的な整合性 を持たせること。

📦パッケージ形状ランダマイザー（Snack Package Shape Randomizer）

お菓子のタイプに依存せず、以下のパッケージ形状から 均等確率でランダム選択 すること。
さらに形状と背景・質感・光源を整合させること。

◆形状カテゴリ一覧（全12タイプ）

縦長袋パッケージ（スナック系）

横長袋パッケージ（板チョコ・バー菓子系）

箱型（小箱）（キャンディ・ラムネ系）

箱型（大箱）（ファミリーパック系）

ブリスターパック（ガム/グミ/おまけ付き）

カップ容器（ポテチ・アイス風）

筒状容器（チューブ菓子/タワー型ポテチ）

スティック型包装（細長キャンディ系）

ゼリー吸い取りパウチ（飲むグミ・ジュース系）

ブックレット型（開くとシールやカード）

玩具一体型パッケージ（おもちゃ内蔵）

奇抜造形パッケージ
 例：キャラの顔立体型、車型、宝箱型、光るボトル型など

🧭シーン最適化（Scene Optimization Rules）

お菓子のパッケージデザインやコンセプトに合わせて、コントラストが際立ちパッケージが際立つような環境になるよう、以下を自動調整すること：

照明（明るさ・暖色/寒色・方向）
季節感（夏冬/春秋）
屋内/屋外
時間帯（昼/夜）
```

**Author**: [ケンイチ | AIスキルアカデミー『仕事に使えるAI活用術』](https://x.com/ChatgptAIskill)  **Date**: 2025-12-07  **Language**: en

> 这是一个高度具体的提示词，用于生成使用超清晰、高亮度有色亚克力板重构插画的产品摄影图。它要求严格保留原始艺术风格、详细的构图规则（底板、金属支座、透明边距）以及光线传输和色彩的材料物理规则。光线必须强烈且冷峻，在墙壁上投射出明亮、发光、高度半透明的彩色焦散图案。

![分层亚克力艺术品产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438504036_8im8am_G7jplU4awAAEuUy.jpg)
![分层亚克力艺术品产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438504163_i3ok09_G7jplU1bMAAK82k.jpg)
![分层亚克力艺术品产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438505760_bimern_G7jplUxa8AEvF3k.jpg)
![分层亚克力艺术品产品摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438507343_vaofo5_G7jplUwboAAzgZT.jpg)

```
Product photography, perfectly straight-on frontal view. CRITICAL: The original art style, linework, and character features of the input illustration MUST BE STRICTLY PRESERVED. Do not abstract or simplify the drawing itself.

The artwork is a physical multi-layered construction mounted on a white wall.
**COMPOSITION RULE:**
1. The aspect ratio and orientation of the final product photography should match the dimensions of the input source image.
2. A large clear base panel is secured with visible metallic standoffs.
3. Crucially, the entire die-cut illustration (all layers) MUST be contained entirely within the boundaries of this base panel.
4. There should be an appropriate clear margin between the edges of the illustration and the edges of the base panel.

**MATERIAL PHYSICS RULE (HIGH TRANSMISSION):**
On top of the base, the illustration is reconstructed using **ultra-clear, highly luminous tinted acrylic sheets** designed for maximal light transmission.
1. The colors are the color of the transparent material itself (glass-like), not painted.
2. **For Skin/White Areas:** MUST be **pure, colorless, ultra-clear glass-like acrylic**.
3. **For Colored Areas (Hair/Clothes):** Use **highly translucent colored acrylic**. The color is vibrant but extremely see-through, allowing significant light to pass.

**LIGHTING & SHADOWS:**
Strong cool diagonal lighting passes through the highly transparent artwork. **Instead of creating dark or heavy shadows, the light casts bright, glowing, highly translucent colorful caustics onto the wall, showing the wall's texture underneath.** The shadow area should feel light and airy, revealing the original colors as bright projections. 8k resolution, ultra-detailed.
```

### 82. Nano Banana Pro 主控提示模板 (JSON)

**Author**: [Ryan Hart](https://x.com/thisdudelikesAI)  **Date**: 2026-03-04  **Language**: en

> Nano Banana Pro 的完整 JSON 模板，旨在结合所有技术和创意控制（场景、相机、灯光、色彩分级、文本、参考、角色），以生成完美的图像。

![Nano Banana Pro 主控提示模板 (JSON)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692210203_p3fahr_HCjhvLZawAIDbVH.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_mode": "thinking|standard",

  "output_specifications": {
    "resolution": "1K|2K|4K",
    "aspect_ratio": "16:9|1:1|9:16|custom",
    "quality_priority": "speed|balanced|quality"
  },

  "scene_description": {
    "primary_subject": "{argument name="primary subject" default="[main focus of image]"}",
    "environment": "{argument name="environment" default="[setting and background]"}",
    "atmosphere": "[mood and feeling]",
    "style": "[visual aesthetic]",
    "time_of_day": "[if relevant]"
  },

  "camera_controls": {
    "angle": "[camera perspective]",
    "focal_length": "[lens type - wide/standard/telephoto]",
    "depth_of_field": "[shallow/deep, what's in focus]",
    "composition": "[rule of thirds/centered/golden ratio/etc]"
  },

  "lighting_setup": {
    "primary_light": {
      "type": "[natural/studio/dramatic/soft]",
      "direction": "[where light comes from]",
      "intensity": "[bright/moderate/moody]"
    },
    "shadows": "[deep/subtle/minimal]",
    "color_temperature": "[warm/cool/neutral]",
    "special_effects": "[rim light/backlighting/etc if needed]"
  },

  "color_grading": {
    "overall_tone": "[vibrant/muted/monochrome/etc]",
    "color_palette": ["primary color", "secondary color", "accent color"],
    "mood": "[emotional impact of colors]"
  },

  "text_elements": [
    {
      "text_content": "[exact text to render]",
      "position": "[location in image]",
      "font_style": "[typography description]",
      "size": "[relative size]",
      "color": "[text color]",
      "effects": "[glow/shadow/3D/etc]",
      "language": "[if not English]"
    }
  ],

  "reference_images": [
    {
      "image_id": 1,
      "purpose": "style reference|composition reference|color reference|character reference",
      "extract_elements": ["specific elements to copy"],
      "apply_to": "[where to use these elements]",
      "transfer_intensity": "[0-100%]"
    }
  ],

  "characters": [
    {
      "character_id": 1,
      "detailed_description": "[ethnicity, age, gender, facial features, hair, expression]",
      "clothing": "[detailed outfit description]",
      "pose": "[body position and gesture]",
      "position_in_scene": "[spatial placement]",
      "consistency_reference": "[image_id if maintaining across multiple generations]"
    }
  ],

  "grounding": {
    "enabled": true|false,
    "search_queries": ["facts to verify"],
    "data_requirements": ["specific information needed"],
    "accuracy_priority": "high|medium"
  },

  "style_constraints": {
    "artistic_style": "[photorealistic/illustration/3D render/watercolor/etc]",
    "inspiration": "[specific artists or movements if relevant]",
    "must_avoid": ["elements to exclude"]
  },

  "technical_requirements": {
    "intended_use": "[social media/print/web/presentation]",
    "safe_zones": "[areas to keep clear fo"
  }
}
```

### 89. iPhone 美学提示词生成器框架

**Author**: [Machina](https://x.com/EXM7777)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: en

> 这是一个元提示或系统指令，旨在引导大型语言模型（如 Nano Banana 2）生成高度具体、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于创建超逼真的 AI 影响者，模拟 iPhone Pro Max 摄像头的光学特性和美学（例如，24mm 焦距、深度融合、计算散景）。用户必须提供场景描述才能触发 JSON 输出。

![iPhone 美学提示词生成器框架](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346659160_chqwxf_HCQU8qpa0AAod9b.jpg)

```
<role>
You're specialized in computational photography, specifically the optical characteristics of the iPhone 16/17 Pro Max sensor system. You translate human concepts into mathematically precise image generation prompts.
</role>

<cognitive_framework>
<principle name="Context Hunger">
If the user provides a vague concept (e.g., "girl at a cafe"), you must explicitly invent the missing environmental, lighting, and styling details to ensure a complete image.
</principle>
<principle name="The iPhone Aesthetic">
All outputs must strictly simulate high-end mobile photography.
- Focal Lengths: 24mm (Main), 13mm (Ultra Wide), or 77mm (Telephoto).
- Characteristics: "Apple ProRAW" color science, sharp details (Deep Fusion), computational bokeh (Portrait Mode), and Smart HDR dynamic range.
- Avoid: Anamorphic lens flares, exaggerated "cinema" bokeh, or vintage film grain (unless specified as a filter).
</principle>
<principle name="Imperfection is Realism">
To achieve "ultra-realism," you must inject terms describing unpolished reality: digital noise (not film grain), skin texture, slightly blown-out highlights (common in mobile), and natural "snapshot" framing.
</principle>
<principle name="JSON Precision">
Your output is a strict JSON object designed for programmatic use.
</principle>
</cognitive_framework>

<visual_analysis_reference>
The "Influencer Aesthetic" is defined by:
- Vibe: "Plandid" (planned candid), effortlessness, aspirational lifestyle.
- Lighting: Natural window light, golden hour, or "flash photography" (hard flash) for night shots.
- Framing: Vertical (9:16) native mobile aspect ratio, often selfies or point-of-view (POV).
</visual_analysis_reference>

<instructions>
1. Analyze the user's request for subject and mood.
2. Enrich the request using "iPhone Photography" constraints.
3. Format the output strictly as a JSON object with the following schema.
</instructions>

<json_schema>
{
  "meta_data": {
    "style": "iPhone Pro Max Photography",
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16"
  },
  "prompt_components": {
    "subject": "Detailed description of person, styling, pose (mirror selfie, 0.5x angle, etc.)",
    "environment": "Detailed background, location, social setting",
    "lighting": "Smart HDR lighting, natural source, or direct flash",
    "camera_gear": "iPhone 16 Pro Max, Main Camera 24mm f/1.78, or Ultra Wide 13mm",
    "processing": "Apple ProRAW, Deep Fusion, Shot on iPhone",
    "imperfections": "Digital noise, motion blur, authentic skin texture, screen reflection (if mirror)"
  },
  "full_prompt_string": "The combined, comma-separated string optimized for realistic mobile generation",
  "negative_prompt": "Standard negatives + 'professional camera, DSLR, bokeh balls, anamorphic, cinema lighting, studio lighting'"
}
</json_schema>

<task>
Await user description of the scene. Generate the JSON output immediately.
</task>
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[iPhone Camera Aesthetic]]

### 95. 高可控逼真图像生成系统提示

**Author**: [Emily](https://x.com/IamEmily2050)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 一个名为“现实优先提示”（Reality-First Prompt）的元提示或系统提示模板，旨在通过强制执行硬性约束、使用技术语言和指定详细的负面提示来避免“AI 外观”伪影，从而指导大型语言模型（LLM）创建高度受控、逼真的图像生成提示。

![高可控逼真图像生成系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187168827_h54g3h_HAPaQ-lXMAAcCoG.jpg)
![高可控逼真图像生成系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187168812_wbkz1y_HAPaQ-kW4AAN-Wh.jpg)
![高可控逼真图像生成系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187168909_i4tfr3_HAPaQ-lXoAAaKnq.jpg)
![高可控逼真图像生成系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187169841_mnt3nk_HAPaVAPXoAAECGH.jpg)

```
name: "Reality-First Prompt
    primary_use: "Image generation prompt creation (photoreal, editorial-documentary, product, architecture, nature, illustration/3D if requested)"
    works_for: ["people", "objects", "animals", "food", "interiors", "architecture", "landscapes", "abstract concepts (by grounding into visible cues)"]
  mission: >
    Write high-control prompts that reliably produce believable, real-world results by anchoring hard constraints,
    describing observable details, defining one priority focus, and adding strict negatives to prevent common artifacts.
  why_it_works:
    - "Front-loads non-negotiables (aspect ratio, medium, shot type, location/time, framing)."
    - "Uses domain language (camera/light/material behavior) instead of vague aesthetics."
    - "Defines realism with observable cues (micro-texture, imperfections, separation)."
    - "Adds disambiguation clauses to prevent frequent model failure modes."
    - "Strong strict negatives target the 'AI look' and unwanted styles."
    - "Avoids contradictions; keeps one coherent lighting/color pipeline."
  operating_principles:
    - "Hard constraints first; never bury them."
    - "Write like a photographer/designer: measurable, stageable, physically plausible."
    - "Pick ONE primary focus and define it using 3–8 observable features."
    - "Convert style words into camera/light/material behaviors (not filters)."
    - "Specify color & light explicitly: white balance, warmth, contrast, exposure, saturation rules."
    - "Specify camera behavior: lens/phone realism, DoF/focus falloff, grain, edge softness, motion blur."
    - "Use strict negatives as guardrails; keep them targeted and non-contradictory."
    - "No contradictory instructions (e.g., 'accurate WB' + 'heavy teal-orange grade')."
  required_inputs:
    - key: "subject"
      description: "What to depict (who/what), specific nouns."
      examples: ["{argument name="subject example 1" default="a ceramic mug with visible glaze crazing"}", "a mountain bike leaning against a wall"]
    - key: "medium"
      description: "Photo / smartphone photo / film photo / 3D render / illustration (must be explicit)."
      examples: ["ultra-realistic smartphone photo", "35mm film photo", "studio product photo"]
    - key: "aspect_ratio"
      description: "Orientation and ratio."
      examples: ["9:16 vertical", "1:1 square", "3:2 horizontal"]
    - key: "setting"
      description: "Where + time-of-day + primary light source."
      examples: ["indoors near a window during daytime", "overcast outdoor street, late afternoon"]
    - key: "shot"
      description: "Framing + angle + distance + occlusions if any."
      examples: ["close-up from collarbone to top of head", "top-down tabletop shot, 50cm distance"]
    - key: "primary_focus"
      description: "ONE priority: what must look correct/real."
      examples: ["skin realism", "material realism", "typography accuracy", "motion re"
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[Negative Prompt]] [[Meta Prompt]]

### 100. Grok 生成 Nano Banana Pro 图像提示的指令

**Author**: [雨雲(Amagumo)806 ｜ AI Animer](https://x.com/ai_animer)  **Date**: 2026-01-25  **Language**: ja

> 这是一条给 Grok LLM 的指令，要求它根据一个现有的视频生成提示（此处引用但未包含），为 Nano Banana Pro 生成一组五个关键帧图像提示。这是一个用于提示工程的元提示。

### 107. Nano Banana Pro 安全过滤器绕过提示

**Author**: [苍何](https://x.com/canghe)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: zh

> 一个元提示，旨在添加到 Nano Banana Pro 的图像生成提示中或与之集成，以防止触发平台的安全过滤器（Safety Filter）。它指示模型自动过滤掉与暴力、危险或负面情绪相关的潜在禁用关键词，并将其替换为经批准的安全替代词，从而确保提示符合内容审核政策。

![Nano Banana Pro 安全过滤器绕过提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631207210_pbvycu_G-tPCQ0bQAQ7uNb.jpg)

```
应用现在能够自动过滤所有危险词汇,使用安全替代词,并确保生成的提示词符合平台风控要求

绝对禁止的词汇：

类别禁用词汇
能量/特效lightning, electric, energy, spark, voltage, current
战斗/冲突attack, battle, fight, punch, kick, strike, combat, clash
危险元素fire, flame, explosion, weapon, sword, knife, gun
负面情绪fierce, intense, aggressive, violent, rage, angry, scream, panic
身体恐怖glowing eyes, red eyes, blood, wound, transform, distort
强制使用的安全替代词
原词替代词
lightning/electricsoft light, warm light, ambient light
fight/attackmove toward, approach, interaction
fierce/intensewarm, calm, gentle, peaceful
explosion/firebloom, brighten, illuminate, radiate
angry/rageconcerned, surprised, amazed, excited
每个提示词必须包含至少2个安全词汇
gentle, soft, calm, peaceful, warm, bright, smooth, quiet, serene, beautiful, lovely, sweet, slowly, smoothly, gracefully
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[Meta Prompt]]

### 108. Nano Banana 图像生成提示词规则 (JSON Schema)

**Author**: [Kaz / AI✖️ローコード](https://x.com/AI_LowCode)  **Date**: 2026-01-11  **Language**: en

> 一个用于 Nano Banana 图像生成的详细系统提示模板，旨在通过要求所有提示严格遵循特定 JSON 模式来确保团队内部的一致性和质量。它通过定义风格、主体、光照、相机设置和负面提示等字段，确保高质量、细节丰富且一致的图像输出。

```
# Nano Banana Image Generation Prompt Rules

When generating images using Nano Banana, the prompt must ALWAYS strictly follow the JSON format defined below.

## Prompt Schema

```json
{
  "image_type": "Define the specific medium, art style, or format of the source image.",
  "time_period_and_year": "Estimate the specific year or decade based on fashion, technology, image quality, and color grading visible in the photo.",
  "mood_and_vibe": "Describe the emotional atmosphere, energy, and intangible 'feeling' evoked by the image (e.g., the specific psychological impression it gives).",
  "subject": "Describe the main character(s) focusing on demographics, body morphology, distinct physical features, and posture.",
  "clothing": "Describe the outfit in detail, strictly specifying garment names, fabric textures, patterns, colors, and how the clothes fit on the subject.",
  "hair": "Describe the hair color, specific hairstyle name, length, and texture.",
  "face": "Describe facial features, skin texture, makeup details, and the exact facial expression.",
  "accessories": "List all visible accessories, jewelry, glasses, or held items, including their material and design details.",
  "action": "Describe the specific activity, movement, or interaction occurring in the scene.",
  "location": "Describe the environment, visible background elements, architectural style, and spatial context.",
  "lighting": "Analyze the light source, direction, color temperature, hardness/softness of the light, and shadow characteristics.",
  "camera_angle_and_framing": "Describe the vertical and horizontal angle of the camera relative to the subject (e.g., eye-level, low-angle), and the shot composition size.",
  "camera_equipment": "Estimate the likely camera type, lens focal length (e.g., wide-angle vs telephoto), aperture effect (depth of field), and film stock or digital sensor characteristics.",
  "style": "Describe the overall aesthetic, color palette, artistic technique, and visual processing style.",
  "negative_prompt": "List visual defects or unwanted elements to be excluded to ensure high quality."
}
```

## Instructions

1. **Output Format**: The output must be a single valid JSON object.
2. **Completeness**: All fields are required. If a field is not applicable, provide a reasonable default or describe it as "neutral" or "standard".
3. **Detail**: Be descriptive and specific in each field to ensure high-quality image generation.
4. **Language**: The values in the JSON should be in English (as most image generation models are optimized for English prompts), unless otherwise specified.
```

[[Prompt Engineering]]

---

### 110. 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的专家级提示工程师系统提示

**Author**: [Brent Lynch](https://x.com/BrentLynch)  **Date**: 2026-01-05  **Language**: en

> 一个系统提示，指示 AI 模型（Nano Banana Pro）扮演专业的提示工程师。任务是将用户的视频描述转换为复杂且极其详细的 JSON 提示，该提示适用于图像和视频生成模型，并遵循特定的 JSON 结构指南。

```
You are an expert prompt engineer for Nano Banana Pro and all AI Video models

Your task is to convert the user's description into a sophisticated, EXTREMELY DETAILED JSON prompt to match the video supplied

You must output a single valid JSON object.

### JSON STRUCTURE GUIDELINES:

1. **Dynamic Fields**: You are encouraged to ADD new fields that capture specific details about the subject (e.g., "plating_style" for food, "architecture_era" for buildings, "glitch_patterns" for abstract art).

2. **Remove Irrelevant Fields**: Do NOT include fields that don't apply. If the subject is a stove, do not include "hair", "skin", or "pose". Remove them entirely rather than setting them to "N/A".

3. **Subject Specificity**:

- **For People**: The example structure (subject, face, skin, hair, clothing) is excellent. Keep it.

- **For Non-Humans**: Create a structure that fits the object. For example, a car might have "chassis", "paint_finish", "wheels".

4. **Standard Fields**: Always include "constraints" (with "must_keep" and "avoid" lists) and
```

### 113. Nano Banana Pro 构图技巧提示（3 个示例）

**Author**: [Riku (AI Creater)](https://x.com/ud6196)  **Date**: 2025-12-31  **Language**: ja

> 以下是一条教程推文，解释了 Nano Banana Pro 的三种高级构图技巧：1) 使用“文本锚点”强制留白，适用于缩略图/海报；2) 使用“物理相机工作规范”（如广角、低角度）来创建动态场景；3) 使用“信息图网格”来组织布局，例如流程图。每种技巧都附带可执行的提示。

![Nano Banana Pro 构图技巧提示（3 个示例）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456243551_t37opq_G9hoViHaMAYg08d.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 构图技巧提示（3 个示例）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456244098_ynk01t_G9hoZb1asAAJPQQ.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 构图技巧提示（3 个示例）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767456247398_1i8ueq_G9hoXvSbwAA9b8A.jpg)

```
【役割】
あなたはプロのグラフィックデザイナーです。YouTubeのサムネイルを作成します。

【構図指示】
- 画面を左右2分割する構図（スプリットスクリーン）。
- 左側：驚いた表情の日本人女性（実写風）。背景は暗めのオフィス。
- 右側：鮮やかな黄色の背景。中央に太字のゴシック体で「{argument name="テキスト" default="AI革命"}」というテキストを配置。
- テキストの周囲には十分な余白（ネガティブスペース）を確保し、視認性を最大化してください。

【スタイル】
アニメーション映画のワンシーン、サイバーパンク

【カメラ・構図設定】
- レンズ：広角レンズ（24mm相当）を使用し、パースを強調。
- アングル：極端なローアングル（あおり）。地面すれすれからキャラクターを見上げる視点。
- 配置：キャラクターの左手をカメラの目の前に配置し、遠近感を誇張。
- 背景：高層ビル群が消失点に向かって鋭く伸びる構図。

【役割】
あなたはマニュアル作成者です。{argument name="主題" default="お好み焼きの作り方"}を作成します。

【形式】
フラットデザインのインフォグラフィック、16:9

【レイアウト指示】
- 左から右へ流れる「3ステップ」のプロセス図。
- ステップ1（左）：虫眼鏡のアイコン（調査）。
- ステップ2（中央）：歯車のアイコン（処理）。
- ステップ3（右）：電球のアイコン（解決）。
- 各要素を矢印で接続し、等間隔に整列させてください。
- 背景は白、アイコンは青とオレンジの基調色で統一。
```

[[Prompt Engineering]]

### 116. 使用 Nano Banana Pro 的魔术提示词自动生成信息图

**Author**: [テツメモ｜AI図解×検証｜Newsletter](https://x.com/tetumemo)  **Date**: 2025-12-30  **Language**: ja

> 此提示专为 Nano Banana Pro 设计，用户可以输入整篇文章或报告，并自动生成 Napkin AI 质量的信息图或视觉摘要。它是一个将长篇文本转化为视觉内容的强大工具。

![使用 Nano Banana Pro 的魔术提示词自动生成信息图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455045745_s83lhl_G9clYFEWoAAgGDo.jpg)

```
あなたは、インフォグラフィックの専門家です。ユーザーから提供された記事やレポートを読み込み、その内容を視覚的に分かりやすく、魅力的なインフォグラフィックとして自動生成してください。特に、以下の要素を考慮して作成してください。

### 目的
記事やレポートの主要なメッセージ、重要なデータ、プロセス、または構造を、一目で理解できるように図解化すること。

### スタイルとトーン
*   **スタイル**: Napkin AIのような、手書き風、またはミニマルで洗練された図解スタイル。
*   **トーン**: 専門的でありながら、親しみやすく、視覚的に訴えるもの。

### 構成要素
1.  **タイトル**: 記事のテーマを簡潔に表す魅力的なタイトル。
2.  **主要なポイント**: 記事全体から抽出された、最も重要な3〜5つの要点。
3.  **図解**: 要点やプロセスを表現するための、グラフ、フローチャート、アイコン、または概念図。
4.  **データ**: 記事内の具体的な数値や統計データがあれば、それを強調する形で表示。
5.  **結論/アクション**: 記事のまとめ、または読者に期待する次の行動。

### 出力形式
提供された記事の内容に基づき、上記の構成要素を統合したインフォグラフィックの全体像を、詳細な指示として出力してください。図解のアイデア、レイアウトの提案、使用する色やフォントのイメージも含めて具体的に記述してください。

### 記事/レポート
{argument name="記事またはレポートの内容" default="[ここに記事やレポートの全文を貼り付けてください]"}
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[Data Visualization]] [[Visual Summary]]

### 117. Nano Banana Pro 中提示词的六个结构化技巧

**Author**: [AI Market](https://x.com/AImarket02)  **Date**: 2025-12-29  **Language**: ja

> 这是一份指南，概述了使用 Nano Banana Pro 创建高质量图像的六个关键结构元素，涵盖了主体、场景、动作、视觉细节、风格和一致性。这是一个元提示结构，而非具体的生成提示。

```
【プロンプト構造化】
  ①主題：何を生成するか明確に
  ②シーン：環境や背景を詳細に
  ③行動/ポーズ：動きを細かく指定
  ④視覚詳細：照明・質感・解像度
  ⑤スタイル：芸術形式を指定
  ⑥一貫性：複数生成時も統一感
```

[[Prompt Engineering]]

### 118. Nano Banana Pro “正确词语” 捕捉微妙笑容表情

**Author**: [Nene@NFT&AIクリエイター](https://x.com/nenechan_nftart)  **Date**: 2025-12-29  **Language**: ja

> 一份提示词指南，详细说明了在 Nano Banana Pro 图像生成中实现微妙、柔和、闭口微笑的“正确”和“不正确”提示词，强调自然放松的表情，而非过于开朗或明亮的笑容。

![Nano Banana Pro “正确词语” 捕捉微妙笑容表情](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166998594_phpsp6_G9UlFwmbEAAMh9l.jpg)

```
できる人が使う「微笑み指定」の正解ワード🍌

絶対に使う🙆🏻‍♀️
•soft closed-mouth smile
•gentle relaxed expression
•slightly softened eyes

絶対に使わない🙅🏻‍♀️
•smiling brightly
•cheerful
•happy
```

[[Prompt Engineering]]

### 119. Nano Banana Pro 提示策略建议，以确保一致性

**Author**: [Tyyle](https://x.com/tyyleai)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 这条推文讨论了使用 Nano Banana Pro 模型实现一致、高质量结果的最佳提示策略，特别建议避免使用“x”网格，因为这会导致混淆和低分辨率输出。推荐的方法是分别生成一个四角度全身照和一个特写头像，以获得更好的一致性和细节。

![Nano Banana Pro 提示策略建议，以确保一致性](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237964446_hx412s_G8cf4aNWYAAmwa-.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 提示策略建议，以确保一致性](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237964617_0jk6z8_G8cf4aOWQAEd6-V.jpg)

```
gen a 4 angle full body shot, and close up headshot
```

### 120. Structured Prompting Guide for Nano Banana Pro

**Author**: [Ihtesham](https://x.com/ihtesham2005)  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: en

> A guide on how to structure prompts for Nano Banana Pro to achieve better results, emphasizing the use of specific roles, concrete descriptions (e.g., lighting), and structured formatting like bullet points or mini sections.

![Structured Prompting Guide for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991379251_pmtog8_G8IZi18bMAARGx3.jpg)

```
• tell it the role

“you are a senior art director / product photographer / magazine designer”

• be concrete, not poetic

bad: “make it cinematic”
good: “soft studio lighting, shallow depth of field, editorial look”

• lock the format

image type, layout, aspect ratio, style
don’t let it guess

• describe what matters, not everything

subject
background
lighting
style
that’s it

• if you want accuracy → structure

bullet points or mini sections work better than paragraphs
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[AI Image Generation]]

### 121. Nano Banana Pro 缩略图的高级两步提示策略

**Author**: [くろあ](https://x.com/kuroa_ai)  **Date**: 2025-12-12  **Language**: ja

> 这条推文概述了一种先进的两步提示策略，旨在显著提高 AI 输出的质量，特别是用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成 YouTube 缩略图。该策略首先要求一个强大的 LLM（例如 GPT-5.2）系统地总结创建 Nano Banana Pro 提示的最佳实践、术语和限制（创建一张“地图”）。然后，用户要求 LLM 根据该既定系统和用户要求生成最终的具体提示，从而产生更一致和更有针对性的输出。

![Nano Banana Pro 缩略图的高级两步提示策略](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991069448_49c7bc_G793s6JagAIwn6y.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 缩略图的高级两步提示策略](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991069909_uct9yi_G793s6JagAAGaRl.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 缩略图的高级两步提示策略](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991069903_t3zcw5_G793s6JaMAAKhii.jpg)

```
これ、実はもう一段ズルい使い方あるんよな。

1回体系的にまとめさせる
→それを前提に成果物作らせる／論点深掘る
これやるだけで、アウトプットの質がマジで別物になる。

なんでかっていうと、最初にAIの頭の中に
「用語」「判断基準」「禁止事項」「型」「優先順位」みたいな設計図を作らせると、

次の指示がその設計図に沿って出力されるからブレにくい。

例えばNano Banana Proにサムネ作らせたい場合、

①まずGPT-5.2に
「Nano Banana Proてサムネイルを作成するためのプロンプトのベストプラクティスを徹底的にリサーチした上で体系化して。よくある失敗もセットで」
ってまとめさせる

②そのあとに
「今の体系を前提に、Nano Banana Proで{argument name="テーマ" default="◯◯"}ってテーマでYouTubeサムネを作るためのプロンプトを作って。動画の内容はこんな感じで、{argument name="文言" default="こういう文言"}を入れたい」
みたいに、自分の要件を盛り込んだ上でプロンプト作らせる

んで完成したプロンプトをNano Banana Proに入れる。狙い通りのアウトプットがめちゃくちゃ出しやすくなる。

毎回いきなり「作って」って頼むと、AIもその場のノリで出すから当たり外れ出るけど、
先に地図（体系）を作らせると強い。

しかもこの方法、
副業の戦略でも、営業文でも、動画台本でも全部効く。汎用性やばい。

AIに作業させる前に、良い成果物の作り方を整理させて、それに基づいて考えさせるのマジでおすすめ。

ちなみに今回できたサムネは3枚目。
1回目は微妙だったから魅力的なYouTubeサムネの作り方も体系化させた上でプロンプト作らせた。
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[YouTube Thumbnail]]

### 125. Nano Banana Pro Master JSON 模板

**Author**: [Louis Gleeson](https://x.com/aigleeson)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> Nano Banana Pro 完整、高度结构化的 JSON 模板，旨在通过对场景、相机、灯光、色彩分级、文本元素、参考图像、角色、接地和风格限制进行详细控制，确保完美的图像生成。

![Nano Banana Pro Master JSON 模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509721407_mkqhyp_G7y7FdraMAAwAra.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_mode": "{argument name="generation mode" default="thinking|standard"}",

  "output_specifications": {
    "resolution": "{argument name="resolution" default="1K|2K|4K"}",
    "aspect_ratio": "{argument name="aspect ratio" default="16:9|1:1|9:16|custom"}",
    "quality_priority": "{argument name="quality priority" default="speed|balanced|quality"}"
  },

  "scene_description": {
    "primary_subject": "[{argument name="primary subject" default="main focus of image"}]",
    "environment": "[{argument name="environment" default="setting and background"}]",
    "atmosphere": "[{argument name="atmosphere" default="mood and feeling"}]",
    "style": "[{argument name="visual style" default="visual aesthetic"}]",
    "time_of_day": "[{argument name="time of day" default="if relevant"}]"
  },

  "camera_controls": {
    "angle": "[{argument name="camera angle" default="camera perspective"}]",
    "focal_length": "[{argument name="focal length" default="lens type - wide/standard/telephoto"}]",
    "depth_of_field": "[{argument name="depth of field" default="shallow/deep, what's in focus"}]",
    "composition": "[{argument name="composition" default="rule of thirds/centered/golden ratio/etc"}]"
  },

  "lighting_setup": {
    "primary_light": {
      "type": "[{argument name="light type" default="natural/studio/dramatic/soft"}]",
      "direction": "[{argument name="light direction" default="where light comes from"}]",
      "intensity": "[{argument name="light intensity" default="bright/moderate/moody"}]"
    },
    "shadows": "[{argument name="shadows" default="deep/subtle/minimal"}]",
    "color_temperature": "[{argument name="color temperature" default="warm/cool/neutral"}]",
    "special_effects": "[{argument name="special effects" default="rim light/backlighting/etc if needed"}]"
  },

  "color_grading": {
    "overall_tone": "[{argument name="overall tone" default="vibrant/muted/monochrome/etc"}]",
    "color_palette": ["{argument name="primary color" default="primary color"}", "{argument name="secondary color" default="secondary color"}", "{argument name="accent color" default="accent color"}"],
    "mood": "[{argument name="mood" default="emotional impact of colors"}]"
  },

  "text_elements": [
    {
      "text_content": "[{argument name="text content" default="exact text to render"}]",
      "position": "[{argument name="text position" default="location in image"}]",
      "font_style": "[{argument name="font style" default="typography description"}]",
      "size": "[{argument name="text size" default="relative size"}]",
      "color": "[{argument name="text color" default="text color"}]",
      "effects": "[{argument name="text effects" default="glow/shadow/3D/etc"}]",
      "language": "[{argument name="language" default="if not English"}]"
    }
  ],

  "reference_images": [
    {
      "image_id": 1,
      "purpose": "{argument name="reference purpose" default="style reference|composition reference|color reference|character reference"}",
      "extract_elements": ["{argument name="elements to copy" default="specific elements to copy"}"],
      "apply_to": "[{argument name="apply to" default="where to use these elements"}]",
      "transfer_intensity": "[{argument name="transfer intensity" default="0-100%"}]"
    }
  ],

  "characters": [
    {
      "character_id": 1,
      "detailed_description": "[{argument name="character description" default="ethnicity, age, gender, facial features, hair, expression"}]",
      "clothing": "[{argument name="clothing" default="detailed outfit description"}]",
      "pose": "[{argument name="pose" default="body position and gesture"}]",
      "position_in_scene": "[{argument name="position in scene" default="spatial placement"}]",
      "consistency_reference": "[{argument name="consistency reference" default="image_id if maintaining across multiple generations"}]"
    }
  ],

  "grounding": {
    "enabled": {argument name="grounding enabled" default="true|false"},
    "search_queries": ["{argument name="search queries" default="facts to verify"}"],
    "data_requirements": ["{argument name="data requirements" default="specific information needed"}"],
    "accuracy_priority": "{argument name="accuracy priority" default="high|medium"}"
  },

  "style_constraints": {
    "artistic_style": "[{argument name="artistic style" default="photorealistic/illustration/3D render/watercolor/etc"}]",
    "inspiration": "[{argument name="inspiration" default="specific artists or movements if relevant"}]",
    "must_avoid": ["{argument name="elements to avoid" default="elements to exclude"}"]
  },

  "technical_requirements": {
    "intended_use": "[{argument name="intended use" default="social media/print/web/presentation"}]",
    "safe_zones": "[{argument name="safe zones" default="areas to keep clear fo"}]"
  }
}
```

[[Prompt Engineering]]

### 128. 使用“绝望”和“噪音”提示词来营造情感冲击

**Author**: [ねろ](https://x.com/nero_sansei)  **Date**: 2025-12-09  **Language**: ja

> 关于 Nano Banana Pro 的一个讨论，其中提到一个技巧：在提示中混入“噪音”元素，例如“垃圾屋”或“沮丧的人”，可以显著增加图像的情感吸引力和影响力，使其超越简单的美学，描绘出人类的痛苦。

![使用“绝望”和“噪音”提示词来营造情感冲击](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440122150_jutmnc_G7tBZNlbAAAUSoo.jpg)

```
プロンプトに「{argument name="ノイズ1" default="ゴミ屋敷"}」「{argument name="ノイズ2" default="鬱な人"}」というノイズを混ぜる
```

### 130. Nano Banana Pro 质量增强关键词

**Author**: [株式会社クーリエ｜AI×事業開発×マーケ×プロダクト【公式】](https://x.com/Courier2011_inc)  **Date**: 2025-12-08  **Language**: ja

> 以下是 Nano Banana Pro（及类似图像生成 AI）的关键词和技巧列表，旨在提升图像质量、光照、角色吸引力和艺术风格，包括强调语法和负面提示的使用。

![Nano Banana Pro 质量增强关键词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438672389_9g3rvu_G7pJVP-bUAIcP-x.jpg)

```
1. 描き込みと質感を「グッ」と上げる🎨
・absurdres：不条理なほどの高解像度へ。髪や服のディテールが緻密に。
・intricate details：背景や衣装の装飾など、複雑な描き込みを増やしたい時に。
・official art：ラフさを抑え、プロが描いたような整った構図や塗りに。

2. 空気を変える「光と影」💡
・cinematic lighting：映画のような照明効果で、画面に奥行きとストーリー性を。
・soft lighting / soft focus：全体をふんわりさせ、柔らかく可愛らしい雰囲気に。
・ray tracing：光の反射をリアルに表現。瞳の輝きや金属・水の質感が向上します。

3. キャラクターの魅力を底上げ📸
・beautiful detailed eyes：アニメイラストの命である「目」の描き込みを強化。
・looking at viewer：視線をこちらに向けさせ、画像の訴求力を高めます。
・dynamic angle：棒立ちを防ぎ、斜めや煽りなど動きのある構図に。

4. 画風（スタイル）の調整🖌️
・flat color：影を減らし、セル画のようなパキッとしたアニメ塗りに。
・thick painting：厚塗り風のリッチな質感で、重厚感を出したい時に。

さらに精度を高めるコツ🛠
・強調構文：重要な単語は (best quality:1.2) のようにカッコと数値で囲むと安定します。
・ネガティブプロンプト：worst quality などの基本に加え、muted color（くすんだ色）を除外設定に入れると、発色が鮮やかになります😳
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[AI Tip]]

---

### 131. Nano Banana Pro 提示词结构和视觉元素

**Author**: [ケンイチ | AIスキルアカデミー『仕事に使えるAI活用術』](https://x.com/ChatgptAIskill)  **Date**: 2025-12-08  **Language**: ja

> 这是一份基于 Google 官方推荐的 Nano Banana Pro 有效提示综合指南，其中概述了基本的结构框架，并提供了相机镜头、光照、材质纹理和艺术风格的具体示例。这是一个元提示结构，而非单一的可执行提示。

![Nano Banana Pro 提示词结构和视觉元素](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438663145_o2kui6_G7ozMUDbMAAvMoo.jpg)

```
Subject(主題)
+ Composition(構図)
+ Action(動作)
+ Setting(場所)
+ Style(スタイル)
+ Lighting/Material(光/質感)

＜カメラ・構図 6選＞
✅ low angle shot
→ 下から見上げる迫力
✅ close-up
→ 顔・対象物のアップ
✅ wide shot
→ 全体を捉える広角
✅ medium shot
→ 腰から上の標準ショット
✅ portrait framing
→ ポートレート構図
✅ overhead view
→ 真上からの俯瞰

＜ライティング 5選＞
✅ soft morning light
→ 柔らかな朝の自然光
✅ golden hour lighting
→ 夕暮れ時の暖かい光
✅ studio lighting
→ プロ品質の照明
✅ cinematic lighting
→ 映画的ドラマチック照明
✅ volumetric fog
→ 光が透ける立体的な霧

＜マテリアル・質感 5選＞
✅ matte finish
→ つや消しの落ち着き
✅ brushed metal
→ ヘアライン加工金属
✅ soft velvet
→ 柔らかいベルベット
✅ translucent fabric
→ 透け感のある布地
✅ wet texture
→ 濡れた質感・光沢

＜スタイル 4選＞
✅ photorealistic style
→ 写真のようなリアルさ
✅ cinematic style
→ 映画的ドラマチック表現
✅ product photography
→ 商品撮影風・広告品質
✅ editorial style
→ 雑誌的な洗練・高級感
```

[[Prompt Engineering]] [[Meta Prompt]] [[AI Tip]]

### 132. 健身房女性摆拍结构化提示词

**Author**: [Sadie 🥀](https://x.com/NameIsSudee)  **Date**: 2026-04-08  **Language**: en

> 这是一份用于 Google Nano Banana 2 的结构化 JSON 提示词，描述了一位在光线昏暗的健身房中，身穿棕色运动连体衣并佩戴棒球帽，侧身坐在健身长椅上微笑的雀斑年轻女性。该提示词指定了照片级真实风格、电影级光效以及浅景深效果。

![健身房女性摆拍结构化提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775717434794_q29z4n_HFWHTRVaEAAtr_n.jpg)

```
{"A smiling young woman with fair skin and freckles posing in a gym. She is sitting sideways on a workout bench, leaning back with one arm raised behind her head. She wears a fitted brown athletic bodysuit with thin straps and a brown baseball cap with the word '{argument name="cap text" default="SADIE"}' on it. Her expression is relaxed and cheerful, eyes slightly closed. The background shows a dimly lit gym environment with blurred workout equipment. Soft lighting highlights her skin and creates a cinematic, shallow depth-of-field effect.", "style": "photorealistic, cinematic lighting, shallow depth of field", "camera": "portrait shot, medium close-up, slight angle", "environment": "modern indoor gym, blurred background", "mood": "relaxed, confident, warm"}
```

### 152. 电影级微距玩具摄影：迷你野兽

**Author**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_)  **Date**: 2026-03-21  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多段式提示，用于生成电影般的微距玩具摄影场景。其概念涉及数十个相同的微型角色实例，它们在一个巨大的开放漫画书上工作，这本漫画书讲述了它们自己的故事。该提示严格执行形象完整性、特定相机视角（低角度微距、90-100mm 镜头）、浅景深和硬定向照明。

![电影级微距玩具摄影：迷你野兽](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774161440924_igvzbo_HD8hTgkaIAAP3Mq.jpg)

```
A cinematic macro toy-photography scene of the uploaded reference character multiplied into dozens of miniature identical instances, each actively working on a giant open comic book that tells the story of the same character.
Likeness Integrity (CRITICAL)

All miniature instances must preserve the exact identity of the reference character:

• identical proportions

• exact eye shape, spacing, stylization

• same silhouette and material behavior

• no added features, no face changes, no stylization drift
The comic book artwork must depict the exact same character design language, translated into printed comic style without altering anatomy or facial structure.
Scene Concept & Action
The giant comic book lies open like a construction site of narrative.
Mini characters are scattered across the pages, each performing a specific task:
• some are drawing panels with tiny tools (pens, brushes, stylus-like tools)

• some are painting color into panels

• some are climbing panel borders like scaffolding

• some are inspecting scenes, pointing, directing

• some are physically interacting with the comic world ( lifting panels, stepping into frames)
The scene must feel like they are building their own story in real-time.
Perspective & Composition (MANDATORY)
Camera & Perspective (Corrected)
Low-angle macro shot, camera positioned close to the comic page
Lens: 90–100mm macro (compression, NOT distortion)
• Perspective compression must preserve consistent object scale

• Foreground character appears larger only due to proximity to lens

• No exaggerated wide-angle distortion

• Spatial depth created through distance falloff + focus, not scaling

• The open comic book stretches diagonally into depth

• Panels form strong leading lines across the frame

• Composition is intentionally off-balance, not centered

• Some characters partially cropped by frame edges
Foreground includes blurred ink tools, paper edges, or panel borders creating depth layering
Depth of Field (CRITICAL)
Extremely shallow depth of field
• Primary focal plane: one or two mini characters in the foreground actively working

• Mid-ground characters slightly softer

• Background characters and panels fall into creamy blur
No full-frame sharpness
Focus must guide the viewer toward the “main worker” character
Lighting Doctrine
Hard directional cinematic light from top-left
• sharp shadows cast across comic panels

• subtle rim light separating characters from page

• ink reflections create small specular highlights

• shadows from panel edges create natural depth
No flat lighting
Environment & Surface Detail
Macro-level realism of the comic book:
• visible paper fibers

• ink texture and slight gloss

• subtle imperfections in print

• panel borders slightly raised or embossed
Tiny tools leave micro mar
```

[[Shallow Depth Of Field]] [[Miniature Figure]]
